Double Zero refers to the semolina flour used in making traditional italian style pizza dough.  I have frequented a few other restaurants who utilize this amazing flour to make their dough and in comparison Double Zero's methods are top-notch.  Their margherita pizza was absolutely perfect.  The restaurant is entirely vegan and among the best I've been to in the LA area<//text>

< Text>
I love double zero, so I am biased. Having been a patron at their NY, RI, and CA locations, let me say this: the team in Venice are absolutely stellar. The food is incredible, so I won't even go on and on about the truffle pizza or tiramisu... But amid this pandemic, the team (and one young lady in particular) in Venice were above and beyond gracious and hospitable and all of the things you would hope for in a service team. I watched aggressive takeout customers get rude with her, and she continued to be polite and courteous. It was a bit of a testimony for how humans should treat one another. All of the staff couldn't be nicer, but to do so in the wake of cranky customers demanding food and demanding it immediately, they delivered deliciousness and manners. Kudos to whoever staffed this location!< /Text>

< Review>
MY NEW FAVE VEGAN JOINT. Who ever thinks plant based items aren't tasty, think again. Double Zero masters vegan dishes, from pizzas to non-pizzas.

I discovered this place with my Off The Menu app (membership app where you get to redeem a free item of food everyday in LA. Check them out!) OTM was featuring Double Zero's Sunflower Caesar Salad and oh my word it's delicious. Made with wood fired croutons and almond parmesan, this salad took me to vegan heaven. I enjoyed it with a glass of white wine *pinky up*

Their pizza selection is also tasty -- i went for the Margherita. My italian roots would be proud. The plant based meatball was excellent as well!

The ambiance and customer service was 11/10.

Overall I really enjoyed discovering this vegan spot and my experience was well worth it! Highly recommend coming here for lunch or even a cute date spot!</Review>

< Review>
Disappointed to give 2 stars when my partner and I were excited to eat their Vegan Pizza. We ordered the ‚ÄúBianca‚Äù for pick up. Kaitlyn explained it‚Äôs a 45min wait which was no problem for a busy Sunday night. We showed up closer to pick up time and patiently awaited what appeared to be online the best vegan pizza we would have. We are low gluten eaters not completely gluten free, we ordered a gluten free crust as a preference. Also ordered the semolina cake.

The restaurant ambience and set is excellent. Kaitlyn was very sweet and kept us up to speed on our order.
When we finally got our order, and reached home in 5 min, famished and excited to eat this pizza, well here is the review

Pros:
Excellent customer service on pick up
Honest about preparation time
Bianca Toppings: Excellent vegan nut cheese on the pizza
Dessert: Excellent ice cream and moistness on top and outer part of the Semolina Cake

Cons
Burnt crust: for gluten free crusts when the edge is burnt almost halfway in from the edge of the crust well it was chewy and we pretty much couldn‚Äôt eat the ends and about an inch from the ends it was a waste.
Toppings: Excessively salty kale, it was over seasoned beyond what you typically get in a restaurant.
Right there with a burnt crust and salty kale the pizza became off putting. Just ate the middle parts out of hunger.
Dessert: Dry flour in the middle of the Semolina Cake

At $21 (pizza) $3 (gluten free) + $11 (cake) + gratuity which we were generous due to service and assumptions it would be great food. Sadly disappointed. Over $35 spent for a dinner that we are still hydrating over today because there was sooooo much salt on the pizza topping.

I also will point out we walked to the sister restaurant first ‚ÄúPlant Food Wine‚Äù and they redirected us to the ‚ÄúDouble zero‚Äù sister restaurant for the pizza as they do not carry pizzas. This is not clear on the website.

From google search Double Zero, or Plant Food Wine and both restaurant sites link to ‚ÄúMatthew Kenney Cusine‚Äù So we figured pizza is served at both. Nope! That‚Äôs what we discovered after a 15 min walk to ‚ÄúPlant Food Wine‚Äù and ended up doing take out from ‚ÄúDouble Zero‚Äù. It was an eventful Sunday Night. When you google it then you have to go breakdown what is served at each  restaurant before you choose to eat here.

Will I eat here again? No
Will I recommend this place? No
Why? well, first impression - no standardized cooking procedures in place and if it‚Äôs a busy night the staff panic and as a customer we felt it and saw it in the products. This is unacceptable for a restaurant that prides itself on being high end serving celebrities.

Sorry Double Zero. Zero flavor pizza.< /Review>

< text>
I first came to Neovision Optometry over 10 years ago, and even though I've long since moved away from San Diego, I always make sure to come here for my annual checkup when I'm back visiting family.

When I first came here, Dr. Yu recommended that I try out CRT lenses. It worked out great, and ever since then I've been happily wearing CRT lenses at night, and being completely free of glasses or contacts during the day. Every year, I go in for my annual checkup and Dr. Yu adjusts my prescription as needed and orders me a new pair.

I've never had any issues with my insurance either (I have VSP).

< Review>
Very disappointing experience. Was not greeted by a rude receptionist who didn't even look up at me. The exam was very rushed and impersonal. I waited for over 2 and a half hours at my appointment with a room full of disgruntled patients who also had appointments. I thought the selection of glasses was very cheap looking. They try to upsell you as much as possible to then pretend that they are giving you some great deal. The staff try to appear to be busy by just walking around and leaving you waiting. I did not get to chose the type of contacts I wanted, they just order whatever they want. I spent almost $400 and I wish I would have went to Lenscrafters, I would've gotten a better deal and nicer glasses. Upon return to pick up my glasses, I had to wait another half an hour just to have someone go get my glasses out of a bin.  I definitely would not recommend this place to anyone and I will take my business elsewhere in the future.</Review>
